**Vault Maintenance\Vault Standards Resolution - 2026-03-31.md** (4 tags)
  - **Content files** (`type: politician`, `sub-note`, `donor`, `pac`, `corporation`, `story`, `daily-update`): A file with any `(UNVERIFIED)` or `(URL NE
  - **System files** (`type: reference`, `methodology`, `index`): The `(UNVERIFIED)` / `(URL NEEDED)` gate applies only to the file's own source citations
  - - `(UNVERIFIED)`, `(URL NEEDED)`, `(API DATA PENDING)` tags are mandatory when data cannot be confirmed
